Pass ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"--no-web"}]," for an API-only daemon."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"One agent process, many clients"}]," — under the default ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"sessionScope: 'single'"}],", every client connecting to the daemon shares one ACP session. Live cross-client collaboration on the same conversation, the same file diffs, the same permission prompts."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Reconnect-safe streaming"}]," — SSE with ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Last-Event-ID"}]," reconnect lets a client drop and pick up exactly where it left off (within the ring’s replay window)."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"First-responder permissions"}]," — when the agent asks for permission to run a tool, every connected client sees the request; whichever client answers first wins."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"One daemon, one workspace"}]," — each ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"qwen serve"}]," process binds to exactly one workspace at boot (per ",["$","$L1c",null,{"href":"https://github.com/QwenLM/qwen-code/issues/3803","children":"#3803"}]," §02). Wraps core’s ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"generateSessionRecap"}]," as a side-query against the fast model; pollutes neither the main chat history nor the SSE stream. Non-strict gate (same posture as ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"/prompt"}],"); SDK helper ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"client.recapSession(sessionId)"}],".\n",["$","ul",null,{"className":"x:[:is(ol,ul)_&]:my-[.75em] x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:list-disc x:ms-[1.5em]","children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Known limit — token-cost amplification:"}]," the route is a pure-cost endpoint (each call is an LLM side-query, no state benefit) and the daemon has no per-route rate limit in v1. On a no-token loopback default a buggy or malicious local client can spam it to burn tokens. ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"generateSessionRecap"}]," reads a snapshot of the chat history via ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"GeminiClient.getChat().getHistory()"}]," and feeds it to a separate ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"BaseLlmClient.generateText"}]," call (via ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"runSideQuery"}],"); it never appends to or mutates the session’s ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"GeminiChat"}],".
